msg:Overall, exceeded expectations.
I took my kids to Disneyland, compared Novotel, and finally chose this one. What I found was a pleasant surprise. I didn't choose Novotel because I was worried that there were too many rooms and the service couldn't keep up. However, this hotel is a boutique hotel with not many rooms, so the service is pretty good. It feels about the same level as the DoubleTree by Hilton. The biggest highlight is the heated swimming pool, which is Novotel in the same price range does not have this.
I booked a business king room for two nights and got a free upgrade to a deluxe king room with a bathtub. The TV is from Xiaomi, it can rotate, and you can watch online TV via screen projection. Good reviews!
What is even more commendable is the Disney transfer, which is a private business car transfer. It is very punctual and considerate, and it only takes our whole family in one car. Every detail of the hotel is good. At this price, the price/performance ratio is unbeatable. It is really a new choice for going to Disneyland.
The only drawback is that the sound insulation of the windows is poor, and the noise from the large cars facing the road is too loud. However, it didn't matter when my child and I fell asleep for two nights. Those who are sensitive must choose a room facing inside.

3. We stayed for two nights in a row and went to Disneyland early the next morning. We then hung up the door sign to ask for cleaning. When we came back in the evening, no one was cleaning at all. When we asked the front desk, the reason was that cleaning was done every other day due to the epidemic. The solution was then A male attendant to clean up? So now that the country has relaxed its policies, your hotel is fighting the epidemic alone? Let a man come into the room in the middle of the night when we are tired from playing all day? I was completely speechless!
4. Breakfast is also mediocre, no different from ordinary chain hotels. It doesn‚Äôt fit the hotel‚Äôs positioning at all!
5. This is the first negative review on Ctrip!
